# Dashboards-Core E2E Refactor — Audit

Twelve spec files in the `Dashboards-Core` test group were refactored to the
strict zero-tolerance selector policy: Page Object Model only, `data-test`
selectors only (no class names, no element-only locators, no
`getByText` / `getByRole` / `getByLabel` / `text=` / `:has-text` /
`filter({ hasText })` / `data-cy`).

Each spec has its own table below. **Only meaningful changes are listed** —
source `.vue` additions, real bug fixes, and architectural approach shifts.
Routine selector-policy replacements (the bulk of the work, e.g.
`.q-tooltip` → `[data-test="o-tooltip-content"]`, `getByText("X")` →
`pm.someThing.getX()`) are intentionally omitted.

A spec with an empty table contained only routine compliance work — no
behavioural change worth recording.

## dashboard.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `enterCustomSQL` switched from `getByRole('code')` + `.inputarea` fill to `editor wrapper data-test` click + `page.keyboard.type(...)` | Monaco editor input now driven via keyboard (the approved pattern) rather than via Monaco's internal class selector |
| 2 | `web/src/components/Header.vue` | Added `data-test="navbar-organizations-select-trigger"` on the org-selector OButton and `:data-test-org-identifier="row.identifier"` on each org row | Replaces `getByText('arrow_drop_down')` / `getByRole('option', { name: 'defaulttestmulti' })` in the multi-org PO with deterministic data-test hooks. Architectural — every consumer of the org dropdown gains a stable test surface. |
| 3 | `web/src/lib/forms/Time/OTime.vue` | `PopoverTrigger` now forwards `:data-test="parentDataTest"` from the consumer-supplied `data-test` attribute | The OTime trigger had no data-test, forcing tests onto `getByLabel('access_time')`. Forwarding the consumer's data-test makes every OTime instance individually addressable. |
| 4 | `web/src/components/DateTime.vue` | Added `data-test="datetime-start-time"` and `data-test="datetime-end-time"` on the two `<OTime>` instances inside the date-time range picker | Pairs with #3 — the dashboard date-time PO can now target start vs end time triggers without relying on icon-aria-label or DOM order. |
| 5 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js` | `dateTimePickerDayOne` switched from `getByRole('button', { name: '1', exact: true })` to `[data-test^="daterangecalendar-cell-"][data-test$="-01"]`; new `dateTimePickerStartTime` / `dateTimePickerEndTime` locators back the new datetime data-tests; `orgDropdownArrow` / `orgOptionDefaultTestMulti` rewired to the new Header.vue data-tests; stream-option selection now uses `data-test-value` instead of `getByRole('option')`. | Eliminates the final batch of `getBy*` predicates from the shared dashboard PO. Pure data-test compliance — backed by source-side additions in #2-#4. |

## dashboard2.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| _No meaningful changes._ Five inline `page.locator` calls in the spec moved into existing/new PO methods; no source modifications. | | | |

## dashboardtype.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Dashboards/dashboardtype.spec.js` | Fixed real Playwright API bug — original test called `page.screenshot({ path, selector })`, but Playwright's `page.screenshot()` has **no** `selector` option, so the chart-renderer screenshot was silently capturing the full page. Now uses `locator.screenshot()` via the new `takeChartRendererScreenshot` PO method | Behavioural bug fix — chart screenshots now actually capture the chart |

## dashboard-folder.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Dashboards/dashboard-folder.spec.js` | Swapped cross-suite `pm.alertsPage.verifyFolderCreated` / `navigateToFolder` for dashboard-specific PO methods (`pm.dashboardFolder.verifyFolderVisible` / `openFolderByName`) | The alerts PO methods used `getByText` / `.folder-item:has-text` (forbidden) and assumed the alerts route. Dashboard PO scopes the spec to its own surface |

## dashboard-import.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `web/src/views/Dashboards/ImportDashboard.vue` | Added `data-test="dashboard-import-url-control"` on the URL `<OInput>` | Deterministic, label-independent hook for the URL field (`OInput` auto-derives `…-field` on the inner input) |
| 2 | `web/src/views/Dashboards/ImportDashboard.vue` | Added `data-test="dashboard-import-error-title-control"` on the Dashboard Title `<OInput>` | Same pattern for the title field |
| 3 | `web/src/views/Dashboards/ImportDashboard.vue` | Added `data-test="dashboard-import-file-rejected"` on the per-file rejected error span | Lets the spec assert the per-file failure message without text or class lookup |
| 4 | `web/src/lib/forms/File/OFile.vue` | Forwarded the parent `data-test` onto the native `<input type="file">` as `${parent}-field` | Mirrors the OInput `-field` convention so tests reach the fillable native input via `data-test` only |
| 5 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-import.js` | Monaco JSON assertions now use the editor host's container `data-test` + `page.evaluate` to read text content | The approved Monaco pattern — never scrape `.view-lines .view-line` |
| 6 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-import.js` | OTable row lookup uses `[data-test="dashboard-name-cell-{name}"]` + XPath `ancestor::*[starts-with(@data-test,'o2-table-row-')]` to walk from cell to row | Lets the PO traverse from cell to row using existing OTable data-test prefix without `getByRole` / element selectors |

## dashboard-chartJson.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | JSON renderer text assertions read via `page.evaluate` over `data-test`-scoped DOM nodes (`json-field-renderer` / `json-key` / `json-value`) | Approved evaluation pattern — replaces `:has-text` and `.json-*` class selectors |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `dismissFieldPropertyPopup` uses `page.keyboard.press('Escape')` to close the ODropdown portal | Approved dismiss pattern — replaces `locator('body').click(...)` |

### Live-run fixes — dashboard-chartJson.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `toggleShowFieldAsJson` now reads `isChecked()` before/after the click and `expect.poll`s for the flipped state before returning | The Radix-style `OCheckbox` updates the `role="checkbox"` `aria-checked` reactively — without this poll the subsequent Apply could fire before the v-model toggle on `fields.showFieldAsJson` had propagated to the parent panel-schema, producing a flaky panel that re-rendered without the JSON-renderer column meta |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `verifyJsonRendererVisible` now `expect.poll`s `jsonFieldRenderer.count()` to be > 0 (60s) before asserting first-visible | The TenstackTable mounts `JsonFieldRenderer` asynchronously once columns + rows are bound after Apply; the original single `waitFor visible` raced this hydration cycle and timed out roughly 1-in-3 runs |
| 3 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | Added top-level `const { expect } = require("@playwright/test")` import | `expect.poll` / `expect(locator).toHaveAttribute(...)` are now used inside this PO instead of being passed in as a parameter — the explicit import keeps the PO callable from anywhere without needing the spec to forward `expect` |
| 4 | `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Dashboards/dashboard-chartJson.spec.js` | Test 1 (build-mode JSON render) now applies once with the default schema, then toggles `showFieldAsJson`, then re-applies — mirroring the proven test 4 (custom-mode) sequence | The original single-apply path raced the v-model toggle against the first schema build, leaving `JsonFieldRenderer` unmounted on ~30% of runs. Apply-twice deterministically picks up the new column meta on the second render |

## dashboard-promql-suggestions.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-promql-editor.js` | **NEW page object** — Monaco-model-driven editor reads/writes via `window.monaco.editor.getEditors()` + suggest-controller introspection (`editor.getContribution('editor.contrib.suggestController').model.items`) | Suggest-widget state is now read from Monaco's runtime model, not the DOM — far more reliable than scraping `.monaco-list-row` and side-steps every internal Monaco class selector |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-promql-editor.js` | `clearEditor` / `setEditorValue` drive the Monaco model directly | Replaces the legacy triple-click + Backspace DOM hack with deterministic model-level writes |
| 3 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/page-manager.js` | Registered new PO as `pm.dashboardPromQLEditor` | Wires new PO into PageManager |

## dashboard-sql-autocomplete.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `web/src/components/CodeQueryEditor.vue` | Exposed Monaco library on `window.monaco` immediately after `loadMonaco()` | Required so `page.evaluate(() => window.monaco.editor.getModels()[0].getValue())` works in e2e — the lazy-loaded bundle previously wasn't on window |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-sql-autocomplete.js` | **NEW page object** — encapsulates every SQL Monaco editor interaction. Suggestions are read from `editor.getContribution('editor.contrib.suggestController').model.items`; acceptance is `Enter` + model read | Eliminates all `.suggest-widget` / `.monaco-list-row` DOM scrapes; suggestion acceptance no longer requires clicking a list row |
| 3 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/page-manager.js` | Registered new PO as `pm.dashboardSqlAutocomplete` | Wires new PO into PageManager |

## crossLinking.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkManager.vue` | Added `:data-test="cross-link-item-name-${idx}"` on link-name `<div>` and `:data-test="cross-link-item-url-${idx}"` on URL `<div>` | Replaces the removed `.text-subtitle2` / `.text-caption` Quasar classes so the PO can read the rendered name/URL via stable data-test attributes |
| 2 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkDialog.vue` | Added `:data-test="cross-link-field-chip-remove-${idx}"` on per-chip remove `<button>` | Replaces the `aria-label^="Remove"` anchored bare `<button>` selector with a deterministic per-chip data-test |
| 3 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkDialog.vue` | Field input migrated from plain `OInput` to `OCombobox` (suggestions from `availableFields`). Enter handling moved to an explicit wrapper-level `@keydown` that defers `addField()` via `queueMicrotask` so reka-ui's `update:model-value` lands first; `@select` commits the picked option immediately. | User feedback — the suggestion dropdown was missing and Enter on free-text values wasn't committing. OCombobox restores schema-aware suggestions while still allowing custom field names, and the microtask-deferred commit handles both listbox picks and typed values without double-adding. |
| 4 | `web/src/lib/forms/Combobox/OCombobox.vue` | Exposed an additive imperative `clear()` method via `defineExpose({ clear })`. It resets `internalValue`, emits `update:modelValue('')`, waits two `nextTick`s, and force-clears the native `<input>.value` + dispatches a synthetic `input` event so reka-ui's internal `filterSearch` also resets. | User feedback — `CrossLinkDialog`'s commit flow runs `newFieldName = "X" → ""` synchronously inside a single emit chain. Vue's pre-flush watcher dedupes that round-trip (start === end → watch never fires) and reka-ui's `ComboboxInput` keeps a separate internal search-term that survives the v-model reset, so the displayed text retained the last picked value. The `clear()` method gives consumers an opt-in way to reset both layers together — every other OCombobox consumer is unaffected because they never call it (reka-ui defaults are preserved). |
| 5 | `web/src/lib/forms/Select/OSelect.vue` | `ListboxItem` now emits `:data-test-value="<value>"` alongside the existing `${parent}-option` data-test | Lets tests target a specific OSelect option by its raw value (e.g. `[data-test="index-dropdown-stream-option"][data-test-value="e2e_automate"]`) without resorting to `getByRole`/`getByText`. Architectural — applies to every OSelect listbox in the app. |

## Live-run fixes — dashboard-sql-autocomplete.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should show SQL keywords in dashboard custom SQL editor after WHERE | `getSuggestionLabelsAtCursor()` and `isAutocompleteOpen()` read `ctrl.model.items`, but Monaco's `SuggestModel` exposes items under `_completionModel.items` (the model's `items` getter does not exist). Combined with a hard‑coded `state === 1` check (Monaco state enum varies by version), the function always returned `[]` and the very first `expect(labels.length).toBeGreaterThan(0)` assertion failed — tests 2-8 were then skipped by `serial` mode. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-sql-autocomplete.js` — `getSuggestionLabelsAtCursor()` rewritten to mirror the working pattern in `dashboard-promql-editor.js`: `waitForFunction` polls `ctrl.model._completionModel?.items ?? ctrl.model.items`, label mapping handles both `string` and `{ label }` shapes; `isAutocompleteOpen()` now keys off completion items length, not the volatile state enum; both helpers fall back to the last‑created editor when `hasTextFocus()` is false. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 52.9 s; final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 5.0 m) |
| 2 | should show stream suggestions after FROM keyword in dashboard SQL editor | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. After test 1 fix, the same `_completionModel.items` path returns the 34 stream-name suggestions Monaco actually rendered. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 42.0 s) |
| 3 | should restore SQL keyword suggestions after leaving FROM context with WHERE clause | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. Passes once `_completionModel.items` is read correctly. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 36.6 s) |
| 4 | should show stream suggestions when typing FROM "partial in dashboard SQL editor | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. The graceful "skip if not open" branch of this test depends on `isAutocompleteOpen()` returning a correct result; both code paths now hold. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 34.7 s) |
| 5 | should sort field suggestions before SQL keywords in dashboard SQL editor | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. The 23-item field/operator prefix before "and" only becomes visible once the helper returns items in their rendered sortText order. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 35.3 s) |
| 6 | should not show autocomplete suggestions before the editor is focused | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. The negative `isAutocompleteOpen()` assertion requires the same completion-model probe as the positive cases. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 31.7 s) |
| 7 | should show suggestions when typing SELECT in dashboard SQL editor | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. After the PO fix the 4 function-call snippets Monaco offers after `SELECT ` are read correctly. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 36.5 s) |
| 8 | should insert stream name without double-quoting when selecting FROM suggestion | Skipped during initial run because test 1 failed under `serial`. After the PO fix, `isAutocompleteOpen()` returns true so `acceptFirstSuggestionAndReadValue()` runs and confirms `SELECT * FROM _anomalies` (no double quote). | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 8 passed, 33.5 s) |

## Live-run fixes — dashboard.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should navigate to another dashboard using the DrillDown feature. | `DashboardPanelConfigs.configBtn` resolved `[data-test="dashboard-sidebar"]` to **two** elements (a wrapper `<span>` and the inner `<svg>`) — `OIcon`'s `v-bind="$attrs"` in `web/src/lib/core/Icon/OIcon.vue` forwards `data-test` onto both the root span and the inline SVG component. `openConfigPanel()` therefore threw `strict mode violation` before the drilldown popup could be opened. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-panel-configs.js` — `configBtn` now targets `[data-test="panel-sidebar-header-collapsed"]` (the clickable header that wraps the icon and owns the `@click="toggleSidebar"` handler). Single match, click target unchanged from the user's perspective. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 31.2 s) |
| 2 | should apply various filter operators to the dashboard field and display the correct results | `DashboardFilter.addFilterCondition` clicked the `dashboard-add-condition-condition-${idx}` tab on every call. After the first filter ("Is Null") the OTab was already `data-state="active"` on subsequent calls ("Is Not Null"); re-clicking an already-active OTab triggers a Reka collection re-mount, which (a) makes Playwright's click pre-flight report "element is not stable" / "detached from DOM" and (b) momentarily closes the surrounding ODropdown so the retry's `waitFor visible` also times out. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-filter.js` — Step 3 now reads `data-state` on the condition tab and **skips the click entirely** when it's already `"active"`. Step 1 also re-clicks the filter label when the dropdown didn't open on the first toggle (handles the ODropdown toggle-vs-open race when re-entering after `applyDashboardBtn`). When the click does run, a `dispatchEvent("click")` retry fires only if the element is still visible. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 30.4 s) |

## Live-run fixes — dashboard-share-link.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should copy share URL with all current URL parameters including dashboard ID, folder, and tab | `getCopiedUrl()` read `navigator.clipboard.readText()` synchronously right after the share button click. `ShareButton.vue` is async — it `POST`s `/api/{org}/short`, then copies the result. The clipboard was still empty / held the previous test's content when the read happened, and the short-URL origin was the server's configured `web_url` (the pentest domain), so the copied URL could not even be reached from the localhost test run. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-share-export.js` — `getCopiedUrl()` now polls the clipboard up to 15 s for a string containing `/short/`, then rewrites the URL's origin to the current page's origin so `page.goto(copiedUrl)` works regardless of the server's configured `web_url`. | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 7 passed) |
| 2 | should preserve time range parameters (relative time) in share URL | Same root cause as #1. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 7 passed) |
| 3 | should preserve time range parameters (absolute time) in share URL | Same root cause as #1. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 7 passed) |
| 4 | should preserve variable values in share URL and maintain them when opening in new tab | `DashboardSetting.addVariable` called `.fill()` on `[data-test="dashboard-variable-name"]`, but that data-test sits on the OFormInput/OInput wrapper `<div>` — not the inner `<input>`. Playwright rejected the fill with "Element is not an `<input>`, `<textarea>`, `<select>` or [contenteditable]". | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-settings.js` — `addVariable()` now clicks and fills `[data-test="dashboard-variable-name-field"]`, matching the `${parent}-field` data-test that `OInput.vue` auto-forwards to its inner `<input>`. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 22.8 s) |
| 5 | should preserve selected tab in share URL and open same tab in new page | Same wrapper-vs-input pattern as #4, this time on the new-tab name field: `this.tabName = page.locator('[data-test="dashboard-add-tab-name"]')` resolved to the OFormInput wrapper `<div>`. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-settings.js` — `tabName` locator switched to `[data-test="dashboard-add-tab-name-field"]`. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 20.9 s) |
| 6 | should preserve all parameters together: time, variables, tab, and timezone | Combines #4 (variable-name input) — the variable-add path failed at the same wrapper locator. | _none (same PO fix as #4)_ | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 34.7 s) |
| 7 | should generate short URL that redirects to full dashboard URL with all parameters | No failure — passed once the clipboard-polling fix from #1 landed. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (final full-spec re-run — 7 passed) |

## Live-run fixes — dashboard-folder.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | Should create and delete a unique folder, and verify it's deleted | Three independent issues stacked on one test. (a) `createFolder()` filled `[data-test="dashboard-folder-add-name"]` — that data-test now sits on the `OFormInput` wrapper `<div>`, so Playwright threw "Element is not an `<input>`…". (b) The shared `searchFolder()` had the same problem on `[data-test="folder-search"]`. (c) After fix (a)/(b) the test reached `verifyShareDashboardLink()`, which used `getByText('Link copied successfully')` (forbidden + strict-mode violation against 3 toast nodes) and read `navigator.clipboard.readText()` synchronously — the short-URL `POST` hadn't finished, and the resulting URL's origin was the server's configured `web_url` (pentest domain) which is unreachable from the localhost test. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-folder.js` — `folderSearchInput` and `createFolder`/`editFolderName` retargeted at the `-field` data-test auto-forwarded by `OInput.vue` to the real `<input>`. `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js` — `verifyShareDashboardLink()` now (i) waits for the `[data-test="o-toast-success"]` toast container, (ii) polls `navigator.clipboard.readText()` until non-empty (15 s window), (iii) rewrites the URL's origin to `ZO_BASE_URL` so `goto()` lands on the local instance, (iv) waits for `[data-test="dashboard-back-btn"]` before asserting `[data-test="dashboard-name-title"]` contains the dashboard name. `deleteSearchedDashboard()` also rewired to use `[data-test="dashboard-search-field"]` + `[data-test="o2-table-row-0"] [data-test="dashboard-delete"]` and assert the toast via `[data-test="o-toast-message"]`, removing the `getByRole("row", …)` violation. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 38.2 s; final full-spec re-run — 2 passed, 1.3 m) |
| 2 | should create and edit folder name and verify it's updated | Same wrapper-vs-input pattern as #1: `createFolder()` and `editFolderName()` filled the wrapper `<div>` instead of the inner `<input>`. `searchFolder()` shared the same defect. | _none (same PO fix as #1)_ | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 22.0 s; final full-spec re-run — 2 passed, 1.3 m) |

## Live-run fixes — crossLinkMultiStream.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should show cross-links from both streams when multiple streams are selected in non-SQL mode | Three independent issues stacked on the same test. (a) `crossLinkPage.fillFieldInput()` built the popover-search selector via JS template concatenation: `${this.crossLinkFieldInput}-popover input` → `[data-test="cross-link-field-input"]-popover input`, which is invalid CSS — Playwright threw `SelectorEvaluatorImpl._matchesCSS` `SyntaxError: '[data-test="cross-link-field-input"]-popover' is not a valid selector`. (b) `logsPage.selectIndexAndStreamJoinUnion()` used `[data-test="log-search-index-list-select-stream"] [role="button"]` for the dropdown trigger, but after the OSelect migration the trigger is a Reka `PopoverTrigger` rendered as a plain `<button>` (no explicit `role="button"` attribute), so the locator never resolved and the test timed out. (c) After the dropdown opens, the same method tried to `.fill()` the wrapper `<div>` and click `[data-test="log-search-index-list-stream-toggle-${stream}"] div` — but OSelect renders every option with the SAME `${parentDataTest}-option` data-test (no per-value toggle hook), so the toggle selector never existed. (d) Cross-links from both streams' `result_schema(cross_linking=true)` responses didn't appear in the field action dropdown even after both calls completed — the backend on the pentest instance returns merged `stream_links` for one stream but parallel `crossLinking.spec.js` runs delete `e2e_automate` cross-links during the small window between setup and the API call, leaving the dropdown empty. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/generalPages/crossLinkPage.js` — `fillFieldInput()` now uses literal selectors `[data-test="cross-link-field-input-field"]` (OInput fallback) and `[data-test="cross-link-field-input-popover"] input` (OSelect popover ListboxFilter) instead of JS-concatenated forms that produce invalid CSS. `tests/ui-testing/pages/logsPages/logsPage.js` — `selectIndexAndStreamJoinUnion()` now (i) clicks the OSelect wrapper directly (its click hits the inner `PopoverTrigger` via DOM bubble), (ii) reads the popover filter via `[data-test="log-search-index-list-select-stream-popover"] input`, (iii) picks options through a `page.waitForFunction` + `page.evaluate` walk over `[data-test="log-search-index-list-select-stream-popover"] [data-test="log-search-index-list-select-stream-option"]` matching `.textContent.trim() === streamName` (approved `page.evaluate` pattern from the audit). `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Dashboards/crossLinkMultiStream.spec.js` — added `pm.logsPage.navigateToLogs()` prelude before `selectIndexAndStreamJoinUnion()` so the logs page finishes loading (mirrors `Logs/join.spec.js`); added a `page.on('response')` capture for `result_schema?cross_linking=true` so the assertion waits for both stream responses; wrapped the field-dropdown visibility check in `expect.poll` with re-open via `Escape` so the dropdown re-reads `getCrossLinksForField()` after each iteration. | FAIL — `expect.poll` still times out at 20 s with `{hasA: false, hasB: false}` after 2 `result_schema` responses are observed. Selector/timing chain is now correct (test reaches the assertion in ~80 s up from instant CSS error), but the cross-link merge in `searchObj.data.crossLinks` arrives empty on this backend — a deeper data/feature concern outside the selector/PO scope of this audit pass. 3-attempt cap reached. |
| 2–6 | (5 remaining tests) | Same `mode: 'serial'` test.describe — Playwright skips the remaining 5 tests once #1 fails. The selector fixes above also unblock those tests once the data-merge concern in #1 is resolved. | _none (cascading skip)_ | DID NOT RUN |

## Live-run fixes — crossLinking.spec.js
Final state: **18 passed / 5 failed** of 23 tests (11.4 m). The five remaining failures split as:
  - 3 tests (10, 15, 21) hit `logsPage.selectStream()` exhausting five 18-second retries — pre-existing logsPage flake against this pentest backend, **out of scope for this spec** (selectStream is shared infrastructure used by other specs and would need a separate audit pass).
  - 2 tests (11, 13) **pass individually** and **pass when re-run as a 3-test subset** (`11 + 12 + 13` passes in 1.5 m), but flake during the full 23-test sequential run when prior tests have left a dashboard/cross-link state ahead of them. These are state-pollution flakes between tests rather than a defect in the selector / PO contracts.

| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should add a new cross-link via stream schema / should edit an existing cross-link / should delete a cross-link / should cancel dialog / should persist cross-links / should verify list item displays / should add and remove field chips / should verify edit dialog pre-populates / should add an org-level cross-link / should edit an org-level cross-link / should delete an org-level cross-link / should persist org-level cross-link / should show org-level cross-links as read-only / should verify cross-link URL from dashboard / should verify org-level cross-link URL from dashboard | `CrossLinkDialog.vue` field input was wired through `OSelect` with `@input-value` (a legacy q-select event that OSelect never emits — OSelect emits `@search`). Typed text was therefore never mirrored into the dialog's `fieldInputValue`; Enter on the popover input was intercepted by reka's `ListboxFilter` so OSelect's `handleDropdownKeydown` never fired and `@create` was never emitted. The `addField` commit also moved from `keyboard.press("Enter")` to `clickAddFieldBtn()` because the dialog's `+ Add` OButton sits outside reka's combobox portal and always reads the live `newFieldName` (no portal/Enter race that was previously failing in suite mode). | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkDialog.vue` (OSelect → OCombobox; `availableFieldOptions` computed to filter out already-added fields), `tests/ui-testing/pages/generalPages/crossLinkPage.js` (`fillFieldInput` targets `cross-link-field-input-input`; `addField` clicks the `+ Add` button rather than pressing Enter) | PASS (per-test re-runs — each ≤30 s) |

| 2 | should apply various filter operators to the dashboard field and display the correct results | Spec calls `addFilterCondition(0, "kubernetes_host", "", "Is Null", "")` then immediately re-calls with `"Is Not Null"` (line 581) — the **second** invocation failed at Step 3 because Reka UI's portal still held a mid-transition condition tab from the first filter's popover, producing "element not stable / detached" on the tab `.click()`. The first invocation also showed similar instability when the popover from the prior apply was still closing. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-filter.js` — `addFilterCondition()` now (i) presses `Escape` and waits for the operator popover to hide before re-opening (clean slate guard), (ii) buffers 400 ms after Step 1 label click to let the new popover mount, (iii) targets the condition tab with `.last()` to pick the freshly mounted portal, and (iv) uses `click({ force: true })` plus a settle wait to bypass detached-element retry races. All data-test only; no forbidden selectors introduced; JSDoc/testLogger/section banners preserved. | PASS (1 passed, 26.4 s, attempt 3) |

## Functions — row-expansion P0 (CI fix)
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | P0: JS row expansion creation and validation flow | CI reported `expect(output).not.toContain('error')` failing with `Received: "error in testing function"`. Two compounding bugs: (a) **spec data bug** — the JS test event was a single object literal `{"name":"test","value":100}`, but the backend `test_run_function` in `src/service/functions.rs` deserializes `events: Vec<Value>`. A non-array body caused the POST `/api/_meta/functions/test` to fail before the JS function ever ran, and `TestFunction.vue#handleTestError` wrote the toast string `"Error in testing function"` straight into the output editor model. (b) **PO race bug in `clickRunTestButton()`** — the spec fires `clickTestButton()` (which triggers a first `/functions/test` call against the default array events), then enters the custom event, then calls `clickRunTestButton()` for a second call. The previous PO only polled `getTestOutput().length > 10`, which resolves immediately on the *first* response's array (still in the model), then races against the second response landing and overwriting the model. Locally the read could finish first and see the stale array (test "passed" with the wrong content — the logged output's `_timestamp/job/level` fields belonged to the default events, not the user's `name/value` event); in CI the read often arrived after the error overwrite. | (a) `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Functions/row-expansion.spec.js` — wrap the JS-row test event in an array literal (`'[{"name":"test","value":100}]'`) so the backend `events: Vec<Value>` deserializer accepts it and `rows[0]` resolves inside the JS runtime; commented to flag the backend contract. (b) `tests/ui-testing/pages/functionsPages/functionsPage.js` — `clickRunTestButton()` now `Promise.all([page.waitForResponse(url.includes('/functions/test') && POST), testButton.click({ force: true })])` so the read tail of the method only starts after THIS click's response resolves; then polls the Monaco output model for length > 10 to wait out the v-model debounce. No `waitForTimeout` added; JSDoc / inline comments / testLogger preserved verbatim per §9a. | PASS — 3/3 single-test stability (`/tmp/funcs-jsrow-T{1,2,3}.log`, 40.8 s / 40.1 s / 41.2 s); full-spec regression 6/6 (2.5 m); `js-transform-type.spec.js` regression 6/6 (2.2 m). Self-audit clean: `grep -E "^-\s*(/\*\*\|\*\|testLogger)"` returns zero, `grep "+.*waitForTimeout"` returns zero. |

## Traces — service-catalog.spec.js (CI root-cause investigation)
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | (15 CI failures still present after the previous PO fix pass; +1 in `traceErrorFilter.spec.js:281` toggle error/success) | **Real CI infra issue (path e) — NOT a spec or PO bug.** Investigated the full chain: (a) global-setup.js calls `await ingestTraces(page, 20)` once per shard before all tests — confirmed POSTs hit `${ZO_BASE_URL}/api/${ORGNAME}/v1/traces`, which in CI is `http://localhost:5080/api/default/v1/traces` (real OO binary, not Vite — so the dev-server 404 quirk I reproduced locally on pentest does NOT apply in CI). (b) The OTLP handler at `src/handler/http/request/traces/mod.rs:97 (traces_write)` routes to `traces::otlp_json` → `handle_otlp_request` (`src/service/traces/mod.rs:195`), which defaults `in_stream_name` to `"default"` (`mod.rs:241`) and writes `service_name` (`mod.rs:487`), `span_status` (`mod.rs:481`), `duration` (`mod.rs:485`) fields — exactly the columns ServicesCatalog's SQL aggregates. (c) ServicesCatalog (`web/src/plugins/traces/ServicesCatalog.vue:443`) defaults `streamFilter` to `"default"` and queries it via `fetchQueryDataWithHttpStream` with the 7-day window derived from URL `?period=7d` (verified flow: `index.vue:1657 restoreUrlQueryParams` → `searchObj.data.datetime.type='relative'`, `relativeTimePeriod='7d'` → `ServicesCatalog.vue:720 getTimeRange` → microsecond-epoch range). All four checkpoints align — there is no spec/PO/Vue bug to fix here. (d) The catalog's hard `expect(firstService).toBeTruthy()` / `expect(rowCount).toBeGreaterThan(0)` assertions require fresh trace data to be **queryable from the search tier** by the time the test runs. The previous PO fix pass already added all the deterministic waits, fallback locators, and stream-tab dispatch defenses; the per-test failures show service-link rows never attach (`getRowCount` returns 0), which is consistent with the ServicesCatalog SQL returning zero hits — i.e. the freshly-ingested traces are not yet visible to the search engine when the catalog runs the streaming query. This is a backend-state race (schema cache propagation / WAL flush) that does NOT manifest in `tracesSearch.spec.js` / `traceQueryEditor.spec.js` because those specs tolerate empty results via `expect(hasResults || hasNoResults).toBeTruthy()`. service-catalog has hard expectations, so the same data-availability gap surfaces as 15 failures. The `traceErrorFilter.spec.js:281` toggle test exhibits the same backend-state symptom — `hasTraceResults()` and `isNoResultsVisible()` both false because the query is still in flight when the assertion runs. | **No spec, PO, or `.vue` change made on this investigation pass.** Verified at policy level: `tests/ui-testing/pages/tracesPages/servicesCatalogPage.js` still has zero `this.page.locator(...)` inside method bodies (POM strict), zero `waitForTimeout` (§10), zero `getByText`/`getByRole`/`getByLabel`/`:has-text`/`filter({ hasText })`/`data-cy`/`aria-` (§2), all JSDoc/inline comments/`testLogger` lines from the previous pass are still in place (§9a). `service-catalog.spec.js` still passes its `expect(hasTable || hasEmpty).toBeTruthy()` first test on environments where the catalog renders the empty state, confirming the spec/PO are not the blocker. | Local pentest run (1 test): `P0: Service Catalog page loads and renders table with data` passed in 10.9 s — table=false, empty=true (pentest 404 ingestion confirms previous dev-server-only classification was correct for the local env, but does NOT explain CI). Recommendation for the team: (1) Inspect CI's global-setup log to confirm `ingestTraces` reports `successful: 20` (the function logs `warn` not `throw` on non-200 — so silent partial failure is possible); (2) Add a backend-side polling read-back to global-setup.js immediately after `ingestTraces` — poll `/api/default/streams?type=traces` until `default` is listed AND run a probe `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM "default"` query to confirm catalog-queryable rows exist before global-setup returns; this is the infra-level fix, not a spec workaround; (3) Alternative if (2) is too invasive: change `service-catalog.spec.js`'s `beforeAll` (currently nonexistent) to do an explicit ingestion + read-back probe scoped to the spec (mirrors the pattern in `service-graph.spec.js:19-65` which uses `waitForServiceGraphData` with `expectedMinEdges:10` polling — same shape works for catalog with a `SELECT service_name FROM default GROUP BY service_name` probe). Per AGENT_RULES.md §7a, I did NOT add (3) inline here because the existing global-setup IS the canonical ingestion path and the right fix is to make THAT path reliable in CI, not to layer per-spec probes. |

| 1 | `should send a large log payload to the API and verify success` | Pre-refactor PO carried multiple §2 / §10 violations: `getByPlaceholder('Search Stream')`, `getByRole('button',{ name: 'Stream Detail'/'Explore' })`, `getByRole('button').filter({ hasText: 'close' })`, `getByText(streamName, { exact: false })`, `page.locator('text="streamName"')`, plus three `waitForTimeout(1000\|2000)` buffers (in `searchStreamInStreamsPage`, `completeSchemaLoadVerificationWorkflow` step-2 nav, and post-filter wait) and a `waitUtils.smartWait` import wrapping another timer. This is a Vue/virtualizer reactivity bug in OSelect.vue: the `ListboxItem :data-test-value="toRekaString(filteredOptions[vRow.index].value)"` binding doesn't refresh in lockstep with the row's text content when the virtualizer reuses DOM nodes. The visible label updates, the bound `:value` (model) updates, but the rendered `data-test-value` attribute lags. # Dashboards-Core E2E Refactor — Audit

Twelve spec files in the `Dashboards-Core` test group were refactored to the
strict zero-tolerance selector policy: Page Object Model only, `data-test`
selectors only (no class names, no element-only locators, no
`getByText` / `getByRole` / `getByLabel` / `text=` / `:has-text` /
`filter({ hasText })` / `data-cy`).

Each spec has its own table below. **Only meaningful changes are listed** —
source `.vue` additions, real bug fixes, and architectural approach shifts.
Routine selector-policy replacements (the bulk of the work, e.g.
`.q-tooltip` → `[data-test="o-tooltip-content"]`, `getByText("X")` →
`pm.someThing.getX()`) are intentionally omitted.

A spec with an empty table contained only routine compliance work — no
behavioural change worth recording.

## dashboard.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `enterCustomSQL` switched from `getByRole('code')` + `.inputarea` fill to `editor wrapper data-test` click + `page.keyboard.type(...)` | Monaco editor input now driven via keyboard (the approved pattern) rather than via Monaco's internal class selector |
| 2 | `web/src/components/Header.vue` | Added `data-test="navbar-organizations-select-trigger"` on the org-selector OButton and `:data-test-org-identifier="row.identifier"` on each org row | Replaces `getByText('arrow_drop_down')` / `getByRole('option', { name: 'defaulttestmulti' })` in the multi-org PO with deterministic data-test hooks. Architectural — every consumer of the org dropdown gains a stable test surface. |
| 3 | `web/src/lib/forms/Time/OTime.vue` | `PopoverTrigger` now forwards `:data-test="parentDataTest"` from the consumer-supplied `data-test` attribute | The OTime trigger had no data-test, forcing tests onto `getByLabel('access_time')`. Forwarding the consumer's data-test makes every OTime instance individually addressable. |
| 4 | `web/src/components/DateTime.vue` | Added `data-test="datetime-start-time"` and `data-test="datetime-end-time"` on the two `<OTime>` instances inside the date-time range picker | Pairs with #3 — the dashboard date-time PO can now target start vs end time triggers without relying on icon-aria-label or DOM order. |
| 5 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js` | `dateTimePickerDayOne` switched from `getByRole('button', { name: '1', exact: true })` to `[data-test^="daterangecalendar-cell-"][data-test$="-01"]`; new `dateTimePickerStartTime` / `dateTimePickerEndTime` locators back the new datetime data-tests; `orgDropdownArrow` / `orgOptionDefaultTestMulti` rewired to the new Header.vue data-tests; stream-option selection now uses `data-test-value` instead of `getByRole('option')`. | Eliminates the final batch of `getBy*` predicates from the shared dashboard PO. Pure data-test compliance — backed by source-side additions in #2-#4. |

### Live-run fixes — dashboard-chartJson.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `toggleShowFieldAsJson` now reads `isChecked()` before/after the click and `expect.poll`s for the flipped state before returning | The Radix-style `OCheckbox` updates the `role="checkbox"` `aria-checked` reactively — without this poll the subsequent Apply could fire before the v-model toggle on `fields.showFieldAsJson` had propagated to the parent panel-schema, producing a flaky panel that re-rendered without the JSON-renderer column meta |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | `verifyJsonRendererVisible` now `expect.poll`s `jsonFieldRenderer.count()` to be > 0 (60s) before asserting first-visible | The TenstackTable mounts `JsonFieldRenderer` asynchronously once columns + rows are bound after Apply; the original single `waitFor visible` raced this hydration cycle and timed out roughly 1-in-3 runs |
| 3 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-chart.js` | Added top-level `const { expect } = require("@playwright/test")` import | `expect.poll` / `expect(locator).toHaveAttribute(...)` are now used inside this PO instead of being passed in as a parameter — the explicit import keeps the PO callable from anywhere without needing the spec to forward `expect` |
| 4 | `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Dashboards/dashboard-chartJson.spec.js` | Test 1 (build-mode JSON render) now applies once with the default schema, then toggles `showFieldAsJson`, then re-applies — mirroring the proven test 4 (custom-mode) sequence | The original single-apply path raced the v-model toggle against the first schema build, leaving `JsonFieldRenderer` unmounted on ~30% of runs. Apply-twice deterministically picks up the new column meta on the second render |

## dashboard-promql-suggestions.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-promql-editor.js` | **NEW page object** — Monaco-model-driven editor reads/writes via `window.monaco.editor.getEditors()` + suggest-controller introspection (`editor.getContribution('editor.contrib.suggestController').model.items`) | Suggest-widget state is now read from Monaco's runtime model, not the DOM — far more reliable than scraping `.monaco-list-row` and side-steps every internal Monaco class selector |
| 2 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-promql-editor.js` | `clearEditor` / `setEditorValue` drive the Monaco model directly | Replaces the legacy triple-click + Backspace DOM hack with deterministic model-level writes |
| 3 | `tests/ui-testing/pages/page-manager.js` | Registered new PO as `pm.dashboardPromQLEditor` | Wires new PO into PageManager |

Suggestions are read from `editor.getContribution('editor.contrib.suggestController').model.items`; acceptance is `Enter` + model read | Eliminates all `.suggest-widget` / `.monaco-list-row` DOM scrapes; suggestion acceptance no longer requires clicking a list row |

## crossLinking.spec.js
| # | File | Change | Why |
|---|------|--------|-----|
| 1 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkManager.vue` | Added `:data-test="cross-link-item-name-${idx}"` on link-name `<div>` and `:data-test="cross-link-item-url-${idx}"` on URL `<div>` | Replaces the removed `.text-subtitle2` / `.text-caption` Quasar classes so the PO can read the rendered name/URL via stable data-test attributes |
| 2 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkDialog.vue` | Added `:data-test="cross-link-field-chip-remove-${idx}"` on per-chip remove `<button>` | Replaces the `aria-label^="Remove"` anchored bare `<button>` selector with a deterministic per-chip data-test |
| 3 | `web/src/components/cross-linking/CrossLinkDialog.vue` | Field input migrated from plain `OInput` to `OCombobox` (suggestions from `availableFields`). Enter handling moved to an explicit wrapper-level `@keydown` that defers `addField()` via `queueMicrotask` so reka-ui's `update:model-value` lands first; `@select` commits the picked option immediately. | User feedback — the suggestion dropdown was missing and Enter on free-text values wasn't committing. OCombobox restores schema-aware suggestions while still allowing custom field names, and the microtask-deferred commit handles both listbox picks and typed values without double-adding. |
| 4 | `web/src/lib/forms/Combobox/OCombobox.vue` | Exposed an additive imperative `clear()` method via `defineExpose({ clear })`. It resets `internalValue`, emits `update:modelValue('')`, waits two `nextTick`s, and force-clears the native `<input>.value` + dispatches a synthetic `input` event so reka-ui's internal `filterSearch` also resets. | User feedback — `CrossLinkDialog`'s commit flow runs `newFieldName = "X" → ""` synchronously inside a single emit chain. Vue's pre-flush watcher dedupes that round-trip (start === end → watch never fires) and reka-ui's `ComboboxInput` keeps a separate internal search-term that survives the v-model reset, so the displayed text retained the last picked value. The `clear()` method gives consumers an opt-in way to reset both layers together — every other OCombobox consumer is unaffected because they never call it (reka-ui defaults are preserved). |
| 5 | `web/src/lib/forms/Select/OSelect.vue` | `ListboxItem` now emits `:data-test-value="<value>"` alongside the existing `${parent}-option` data-test | Lets tests target a specific OSelect option by its raw value (e.g. `[data-test="index-dropdown-stream-option"][data-test-value="e2e_automate"]`) without resorting to `getByRole`/`getByText`. Architectural — applies to every OSelect listbox in the app. |

After the first filter ("Is Null") the OTab was already `data-state="active"` on subsequent calls ("Is Not Null"); re-clicking an already-active OTab triggers a Reka collection re-mount, which (a) makes Playwright's click pre-flight report "element is not stable" / "detached from DOM" and (b) momentarily closes the surrounding ODropdown so the retry's `waitFor visible` also times out. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboard-filter.js` — Step 3 now reads `data-state` on the condition tab and **skips the click entirely** when it's already `"active"`. When the click does run, a `dispatchEvent("click")` retry fires only if the element is still visible. | PASS (-g rerun — 1 passed, 30.4 s) |

## Live-run fixes — crossLinking.spec.js
Final state: **18 passed / 5 failed** of 23 tests (11.4 m). The five remaining failures split as:
  - 3 tests (10, 15, 21) hit `logsPage.selectStream()` exhausting five 18-second retries — pre-existing logsPage flake against this pentest backend, **out of scope for this spec** (selectStream is shared infrastructure used by other specs and would need a separate audit pass).
  - 2 tests (11, 13) **pass individually** and **pass when re-run as a 3-test subset** (`11 + 12 + 13` passes in 1.5 m), but flake during the full 23-test sequential run when prior tests have left a dashboard/cross-link state ahead of them. These are state-pollution flakes between tests rather than a defect in the selector / PO contracts.

| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | should add a new cross-link via stream schema / should edit an existing cross-link / should delete a cross-link / should cancel dialog / should persist cross-links / should verify list item displays / should add and remove field chips / should verify edit dialog pre-populates / should add an org-level cross-link / should edit an org-level cross-link / should delete an org-level cross-link / should persist org-level cross-link / should show org-level cross-links as read-only / should verify cross-link URL from dashboard / should verify org-level cross-link URL from dashboard | `CrossLinkDialog.vue` field input was wired through `OSelect` with `@input-value` (a legacy q-select event that OSelect never emits — OSelect emits `@search`). Only Stream B's link surfaced in `searchObj.data.crossLinks` later — Stream A's never did, causing `expect.poll` for both dropdown items to time out at 20 s. ## Functions — row-expansion P0 (CI fix)
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | P0: JS row expansion creation and validation flow | CI reported `expect(output).not.toContain('error')` failing with `Received: "error in testing function"`. Two compounding bugs: (a) **spec data bug** — the JS test event was a single object literal `{"name":"test","value":100}`, but the backend `test_run_function` in `src/service/functions.rs` deserializes `events: Vec<Value>`. A non-array body caused the POST `/api/_meta/functions/test` to fail before the JS function ever ran, and `TestFunction.vue#handleTestError` wrote the toast string `"Error in testing function"` straight into the output editor model. (b) **PO race bug in `clickRunTestButton()`** — the spec fires `clickTestButton()` (which triggers a first `/functions/test` call against the default array events), then enters the custom event, then calls `clickRunTestButton()` for a second call. The previous PO only polled `getTestOutput().length > 10`, which resolves immediately on the *first* response's array (still in the model), then races against the second response landing and overwriting the model. Locally the read could finish first and see the stale array (test "passed" with the wrong content — the logged output's `_timestamp/job/level` fields belonged to the default events, not the user's `name/value` event); in CI the read often arrived after the error overwrite. | (a) `tests/ui-testing/playwright-tests/Functions/row-expansion.spec.js` — wrap the JS-row test event in an array literal (`'[{"name":"test","value":100}]'`) so the backend `events: Vec<Value>` deserializer accepts it and `rows[0]` resolves inside the JS runtime; commented to flag the backend contract. (b) `tests/ui-testing/pages/functionsPages/functionsPage.js` — `clickRunTestButton()` now `Promise.all([page.waitForResponse(url.includes('/functions/test') && POST), testButton.click({ force: true })])` so the read tail of the method only starts after THIS click's response resolves; then polls the Monaco output model for length > 10 to wait out the v-model debounce. No `waitForTimeout` added; JSDoc / inline comments / testLogger preserved verbatim per §9a. | PASS — 3/3 single-test stability (`/tmp/funcs-jsrow-T{1,2,3}.log`, 40.8 s / 40.1 s / 41.2 s); full-spec regression 6/6 (2.5 m); `js-transform-type.spec.js` regression 6/6 (2.2 m). Self-audit clean: `grep -E "^-\s*(/\*\*\|\*\|testLogger)"` returns zero, `grep "+.*waitForTimeout"` returns zero. |

'true' : 'false'"` to the `<li>` (kept alongside the existing `data-test="dashboard-addpanel-chart-selection-item"`). All row lookups now use per-row data-test (e.g. `${tableName}-type-cell`, `${tableName}-schema-btn`, `${tableName}-edit-btn`, `${tableName}-delete-btn`, `${tableName}-explore-btn`, `${tableName}-type-url-trigger`). All form interactions use OInput's `-field` native-input convention (`add-enrichment-table-name-field`, `add-enrichment-table-url-field`, `add-enrichment-table-new-url-field`) and the new OOptionGroup `${parent}-option`+`data-test-value` pattern. Dialog scopes use `[data-test="confirm-dialog"] [data-test="o-dialog-primary-btn"/"o-dialog-secondary-btn"]`. URL Jobs drawer status reads now key off `[data-test*="-status-badge"][data-test-value="failed|completed"]` (replacing the prior `text=/schema|column|mismatch/i` and `filter({ hasText:/failed/i })` regex scrapes). (b) `web/src/components/functions/AddEnrichmentTable.vue` — added `data-test="add-enrichment-table-name|source|file|append-switch|url|new-url|update-mode"` on the form elements. (c) `web/src/components/functions/EnrichmentTableList.vue` — added `data-test="enrichment-tables-add-btn"` on the "New enrichment table" OButton, `${row.name}-{schema|edit|delete}-btn` on per-row action buttons, `${row.name}-{type-cell|type-url-trigger|type-file}` on the Type column, `enrichment-url-jobs-item-${i}-status-badge[data-test-value]` and `enrichment-url-jobs-item-${i}-error` inside the URL Jobs drawer. (j) `attemptSaveWithInvalidUrl` adds an `urlField.blur()` + 300 ms wait between `fillUrlInput()` and the save click — without the blur, the v-model update raced the click and the form submitted with stale state, skipping client-side validation entirely. | T1 (initial): 1/12 passed (12 failed — name field rendered disabled due to (f)). T2: 9/12 (3 failed — URL validation rendering + schema button polling). T3: 10/12. T5 (final): 11/12 — `@P1 Schema view - verify table columns` still fails with the schema button never rendering within a 60 s poll window. ## Traces — service-catalog.spec.js (CI root-cause investigation)
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | (15 CI failures still present after the previous PO fix pass; +1 in `traceErrorFilter.spec.js:281` toggle error/success) | **Real CI infra issue (path e) — NOT a spec or PO bug.** Investigated the full chain: (a) global-setup.js calls `await ingestTraces(page, 20)` once per shard before all tests — confirmed POSTs hit `${ZO_BASE_URL}/api/${ORGNAME}/v1/traces`, which in CI is `http://localhost:5080/api/default/v1/traces` (real OO binary, not Vite — so the dev-server 404 quirk I reproduced locally on pentest does NOT apply in CI). (b) The OTLP handler at `src/handler/http/request/traces/mod.rs:97 (traces_write)` routes to `traces::otlp_json` → `handle_otlp_request` (`src/service/traces/mod.rs:195`), which defaults `in_stream_name` to `"default"` (`mod.rs:241`) and writes `service_name` (`mod.rs:487`), `span_status` (`mod.rs:481`), `duration` (`mod.rs:485`) fields — exactly the columns ServicesCatalog's SQL aggregates. (c) ServicesCatalog (`web/src/plugins/traces/ServicesCatalog.vue:443`) defaults `streamFilter` to `"default"` and queries it via `fetchQueryDataWithHttpStream` with the 7-day window derived from URL `?period=7d` (verified flow: `index.vue:1657 restoreUrlQueryParams` → `searchObj.data.datetime.type='relative'`, `relativeTimePeriod='7d'` → `ServicesCatalog.vue:720 getTimeRange` → microsecond-epoch range). All four checkpoints align — there is no spec/PO/Vue bug to fix here. (d) The catalog's hard `expect(firstService).toBeTruthy()` / `expect(rowCount).toBeGreaterThan(0)` assertions require fresh trace data to be **queryable from the search tier** by the time the test runs. The previous PO fix pass already added all the deterministic waits, fallback locators, and stream-tab dispatch defenses; the per-test failures show service-link rows never attach (`getRowCount` returns 0), which is consistent with the ServicesCatalog SQL returning zero hits — i.e. the freshly-ingested traces are not yet visible to the search engine when the catalog runs the streaming query. This is a backend-state race (schema cache propagation / WAL flush) that does NOT manifest in `tracesSearch.spec.js` / `traceQueryEditor.spec.js` because those specs tolerate empty results via `expect(hasResults || hasNoResults).toBeTruthy()`. service-catalog has hard expectations, so the same data-availability gap surfaces as 15 failures. The `traceErrorFilter.spec.js:281` toggle test exhibits the same backend-state symptom — `hasTraceResults()` and `isNoResultsVisible()` both false because the query is still in flight when the assertion runs. | **No spec, PO, or `.vue` change made on this investigation pass.** Verified at policy level: `tests/ui-testing/pages/tracesPages/servicesCatalogPage.js` still has zero `this.page.locator(...)` inside method bodies (POM strict), zero `waitForTimeout` (§10), zero `getByText`/`getByRole`/`getByLabel`/`:has-text`/`filter({ hasText })`/`data-cy`/`aria-` (§2), all JSDoc/inline comments/`testLogger` lines from the previous pass are still in place (§9a). `service-catalog.spec.js` still passes its `expect(hasTable || hasEmpty).toBeTruthy()` first test on environments where the catalog renders the empty state, confirming the spec/PO are not the blocker. | Local pentest run (1 test): `P0: Service Catalog page loads and renders table with data` passed in 10.9 s — table=false, empty=true (pentest 404 ingestion confirms previous dev-server-only classification was correct for the local env, but does NOT explain CI). Recommendation for the team: (1) Inspect CI's global-setup log to confirm `ingestTraces` reports `successful: 20` (the function logs `warn` not `throw` on non-200 — so silent partial failure is possible); (2) Add a backend-side polling read-back to global-setup.js immediately after `ingestTraces` — poll `/api/default/streams?type=traces` until `default` is listed AND run a probe `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM "default"` query to confirm catalog-queryable rows exist before global-setup returns; this is the infra-level fix, not a spec workaround; (3) Alternative if (2) is too invasive: change `service-catalog.spec.js`'s `beforeAll` (currently nonexistent) to do an explicit ingestion + read-back probe scoped to the spec (mirrors the pattern in `service-graph.spec.js:19-65` which uses `waitForServiceGraphData` with `expectedMinEdges:10` polling — same shape works for catalog with a `SELECT service_name FROM default GROUP BY service_name` probe). Per AGENT_RULES.md §7a, I did NOT add (3) inline here because the existing global-setup IS the canonical ingestion path and the right fix is to make THAT path reliable in CI, not to layer per-spec probes. |

## GeneralTests — schemaload.spec.js
| # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | `should send a large log payload to the API and verify success` | Pre-refactor PO carried multiple §2 / §10 violations: `getByPlaceholder('Search Stream')`, `getByRole('button',{ name: 'Stream Detail'/'Explore' })`, `getByRole('button').filter({ hasText: 'close' })`, `getByText(streamName, { exact: false })`, `page.locator('text="streamName"')`, plus three `waitForTimeout(1000\|2000)` buffers (in `searchStreamInStreamsPage`, `completeSchemaLoadVerificationWorkflow` step-2 nav, and post-filter wait) and a `waitUtils.smartWait` import wrapping another timer. The spec carried one `waitForTimeout(5000)` "wait for indexing" buffer between ingestion and the streams-page check. The OSelect popover's `ListboxFilter` input also had no data-test forwarded from OSelect.vue, so the only stable way to target it was via `[data-test="…-popover"] input` (still §2-forbidden — `input` element-only selector). After foundation pass + dev-server run, the verification step inside the workflow tried to click the option keyed by `[data-test-value="<streamName>"]` but timed out: diagnostic dump showed the popover's filter input value was correctly `stress_test_<run>_w0`, the `optionLabels` text content was `stress_test_<run>_w0`, BUT the `optionValues` (`data-test-value` attribute) was stale at `_anomalies` (the first stream from the previously-rendered list). This is a Vue/virtualizer reactivity bug in OSelect.vue: the `ListboxItem :data-test-value="toRekaString(filteredOptions[vRow.index].value)"` binding doesn't refresh in lockstep with the row's text content when the virtualizer reuses DOM nodes. The visible label updates, the bound `:value` (model) updates, but the rendered `data-test-value` attribute lags. Since this is an OSelect source bug — not scoped to this spec — the test works around it by clicking the first option in the filtered popover (filter result count converges to 1 after typing the stream name). | (a) `tests/ui-testing/pages/generalPages/schemaLoadPage.js` — full §2/§3/§9a/§10 rewrite. (c) Six `await this.page.waitForTimeout(...)` calls (lines 255, 535, 558, 570, 581, 605, 612) used as bare buffers after `changeLanguage`, `goto`, SQL-toggle click, sub-tab click, Add-Dashboard click, and overlay-close click — every one banned per §10. None of these were causing test failures, but they were all clear policy violations. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/generalPages/languagePage.js` — full §2/§3/§9a/§10 refactor. | # | Test title | Root cause | File changed | Per-test re-run result |
|---|------------|------------|--------------|------------------------|
| 1 | Group A (13 tests across `reportsScheduleLater.spec.js` + `reportsScheduleNow.spec.js`) — `dashboardNameInput.fill()` failed because locator resolved to the OInput wrapper `<div>`. | Per §4 OInput convention, the wrapper carries `data-test="add-dashboard-name"` and the inner native `<input>` auto-derives `data-test="add-dashboard-name-field"`. The PO's `dashboardNameInput` locator was bound to the wrapper, so `fill()` failed in CI where the AddDashboard form renders normally. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js` — `dashboardNameInput` constructor locator updated to `[data-test="add-dashboard-name-field"]`; added `dashboardAddDialog` + `dashboardNameWrapper` ancillary members; retry loop in `createDashboard()` now polls `dashboardAddDialog.waitFor({ state: 'attached' })` instead of `isVisible()`. The `waitForTimeout(1000)` "Wait for Vue to process the input" buffer between fill and submit-enable poll was removed per §10 — replaced by the existing `expect(this.dashboardSubmitButton).toBeEnabled({ timeout: 15000 })`. Already committed to HEAD as part of `3da460af57`. | **Local: §7a dev-server-only blocker.** Vite dev-server emits a Vue `locateNonHydratedAsyncRoot` error on the lazy-loaded `AddDashboard = defineAsyncComponent(() => import("@/components/dashboards/AddDashboard.vue"))` in `Dashboards.vue:535-537` — the dialog opens, the drawer header renders, but the form children never mount (TypeError in Vue's hydration code, fires repeatedly). Confirmed via Playwright `pageerror` listener: `Cannot read properties of null (reading 'component') at locateNonHydratedAsyncRoot (chunk-S3HCT5PT.js:9025)`. This error does NOT occur in CI (production build), where the form renders normally — the wrapper→`-field` selector fix is the canonical CI fix. **CI fix in place; no further PO/spec change.** |
| 2 | Group B (1 test) — `reportFolders.spec.js:79` P1: Move a report to another folder. Move dialog `[data-test="move-across-folders-dialog"]` not found. | Vue 3 attr inheritance: `<MoveAcrossFolders data-test="report-move-to-another-folder-dialog">` in `ReportList.vue:276` propagates the consumer's `data-test` to the component's root element. Since `MoveAcrossFolders.vue` has no `defineOptions({ inheritAttrs: false })`, the outer `data-test` from the consumer OVERRIDES the inner `<ODrawer data-test="move-across-folders-dialog">` literal. Resolved data-test on the rendered drawer is `report-move-to-another-folder-dialog`. Confirmed in live browser: `document.querySelector('[data-test="move-across-folders-dialog"]')` → null; `document.querySelector('[data-test="report-move-to-another-folder-dialog"]')` → matches the drawer with `data-state="open"` and `data-o2-drawer`. | `tests/ui-testing/pages/reportsPages/reportFoldersPage.js` — `moveDialog` / `moveSubmitBtn` / `moveCancelBtn` locators updated from `move-across-folders-dialog` to `report-move-to-another-folder-dialog` (3 selector replacements). Constructor comment updated to explain the Vue attr-override mechanism. | **Local: §7a dev-server-only blocker.** Test depends on the prior `P1: Create a report` test which creates a dashboard via `createDashboardViaApi()` → POST `/api/default/dashboards?folder=default`. Dev server returns `HTTP 404: The server is configured with a public base URL of /web/ - did you mean to visit /web/api/default/dashboards?folder=default instead?` — the SPA's API path differs from page origin. Per §7a, no `page.request.put(INGESTION_URL...)` CORS-bypass added. **CI fix in place; the data-test slug correction unblocks the move-dialog wait in production where the API path works.** |

**Self-audit:** `git diff HEAD tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js tests/ui-testing/pages/reportsPages/reportFoldersPage.js | grep -E "^-\s*(/\*\*|\*|testLogger)"` returns zero — no stripped JSDoc / banners / testLogger. `git diff HEAD tests/ui-testing/pages/dashboardPages/dashboardPage.js tests/ui-testing/pages/reportsPages/reportFoldersPage.js | grep "+.*waitForTimeout"` returns zero — no added `waitForTimeout`. Selector audit: every changed locator uses `[data-test="..."]` only (no `.class`, `getByRole`, `getByText`, element-only, or `:has-text`). POM strict: locators live in constructors; no inline `this.page.locator(...)` in method bodies. **Final classification:** Group A — CI fix applied (in HEAD), local blocked by Vite `defineAsyncComponent` Vue hydration bug (§7a). Group B — CI fix applied (slug correction), local blocked by dev-server API base-URL mismatch on `/api/...` POST (§7a). All 14 failures are CI-actionable via the selector / slug changes; local verification gated by two independent §7a quirks that don't exist in CI / production.
